msg:Very beautiful hotel (attached with the hotel back garden scenery map for reference), in the current area is very eye-catching, standing on the Huixian Pavilion of the Eight Immortals Crossing the Sea can also be seen at a glance. I stayed in Yiyue Building, the room is spacious, the bathroom is separated from the bathing and washing basin on the left and right sides of the entrance, I like this layout, the family can staggered use, more time-saving. The hotel is very close to the scenic area, about 1 km away from Penglai Pavilion and the Eight Immortals Crossing the Sea, Sanxian Mountain. It is not far to the Polar Ocean World and the Europa Park. The hotel can also be booked to go to Changdao. There are some attractions nearby. Turn right and you will see the beach about 100 meters away. The location is excellent. You can go out to the Baolong Commercial Street opposite for eating and shopping. The hotel has a restaurant open all day, and you can also order room service. The hotel will even send someone to deliver the guests' takeaway to the room. The service is simply too good. Check-in and check-out were very efficient. The front desk beauty and a handsome boy worked perfectly together. I got the room card quickly and took the initiative to introduce all the questions I would ask before each check-in. The lobby manager also took the initiative to help when he saw the elderly. All the front office staff, including the young doorman, the travel reservation guy at the door, and the security brother and uncle outside the door were very enthusiastic and kind, giving people a homely feeling. They answered all questions, always greeted with a smile, and took the initiative to introduce. We found that we bought a large bucket of water in the room and had a large demand for water. After that, we put several more bottles of water every day. They were very attentive and thoughtful. The front desk provided free lemonade and freshly ground coffee all day, and there was even free seagull food. The seagull food was too luxurious, and I couldn't bear to get it later. It was so thoughtful for the guests staying in the hotel. The seagulls were all rushing to eat it. I stayed for a few days and had a good time eating, drinking and playing. If I have the opportunity in the future, I will choose to stay at this hotel again. I would also like to thank Tina in the front office. I bothered her several times and was very patient and efficient.
